### [143] [ToolPrivacyBench: Benchmarking Purpose-Bound Privacy in Tool-Using LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28061)
*Shijing Hu,Liang Liu,Zhu Meng,Zhicheng Zhao*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: ToolPrivacyBench提出了一个评估LLM智能体在多工具调用过程中隐私过度泄露的基准，包含2150个案例，发现任务成功执行并不等同于隐私合规。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有功能调用基准主要评估任务完成度和API正确性，而隐私评估基准仅关注最终响应或隐私判断，两者都无法捕获跨多工具轨迹的、与目的绑定的信息流，因此需要一个新的评估视角。

Method: 构建2150个案例（含1150个合成隐私敏感工作流和1000个改编案例），每个案例配有策略知识库；智能体执行后，评估器将记录的工具参数和后端审计日志与策略知识库对比，检测隐私过度披露。

Result: 在9种广泛使用的智能体上测试，发现成功的工具执行并不等同于恰当的隐私披露：智能体可能在完成任务的同时，通过中间工具调用传输了不必要的隐私信息。

Conclusion: 提出"按需知晓"的披露边界（每个工具只应接收其目的所需信息），并通过轨迹级审计来识别多工具工作流中的隐私过度泄露。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have increasingly moved from standalone text generation systems to agents that invoke external tools, access environments, and execute multi-step tasks. However, conventional function-calling benchmarks mainly evaluate task completion and API correctness, while privacy evaluation benchmarks typically focus on final responses or privacy judgments. Neither perspective captures purpose-bound information flow across an executed multi-tool trajectory. Motivated by this limitation in current agent evaluation, ToolPrivacyBench audits whether task-private atoms are routed only to authorized tools and downstream sinks, thereby evaluating both task completion and privacy over-disclosure during tool use. The benchmark contains 2,150 cases, including 1,150 fully synthetic privacy-sensitive business workflows and 1,000 cases adapted from existing multi-tool and function-calling benchmarks. Each case is represented by a policy knowledge base. After an agent executes against mock business backends, the evaluator compares recorded tool arguments and backend audit logs with this policy knowledge base. The evaluation covers nine widely used agents to characterize purpose-bound privacy over-disclosure. The results show that successful tool execution does not imply appropriate privacy disclosure: an agent may complete a task while transmitting unnecessary private information through intermediate tool calls. ToolPrivacyBench therefore formalizes a need-to-know disclosure boundary, under which each tool should receive only the information necessary for its stated purpose, and uses trajectory-level auditing to identify privacy over-disclosure in multi-tool workflows.

### [144] [GTI-mSEMP Framework : A Proposed Framework to Stimulate Malware Propagation with Inclusion of Attacker-Defender Strategy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28079)
*Shadeeb Hossain,Kristopher Wilson*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文提出GTI-mSEMP框架，将博弈论整合到无线传感器流行病恶意软件传播模型中，分析攻防双方在不称称网络环境下的动态博弈与恶意软件传播规律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统流行病学模型将安全防御视为静态参数，无法捕捉攻防双方之间的战略性与不对称博弈，难以适用于资源受限的异构网络环境。

Method: 提出博弈论集成的改进型多无线传感器流行病恶意软件传播（GTI-mSEMP）框架，通过数值模拟分析三种运行机制（均衡对抗、利用激增、强化防御）下易感（S）和恢复（R）节点群体的动态轨迹。

Result: 数值模拟展示了网络状态变量的实时瞬态动力学，揭示了当防御或攻击缩放向量具有效率优势时流行病曲线的变化规律。

Conclusion: 该数学与数值框架可在高度对抗性网络环境中评估动态恶意软件传播，预测局部节点种群状态，为动态防御决策提供理论基础。

Abstract: The rapid proliferation of automated, multi-vector malware threats poses a significant risk to heterogeneous, resource constrained cyber-physical networks. Conventional epidemiological models often treat security defenses as static parameters, failing to capture the strategic, asymmetric maneuvers between an attacker and a defender. To address the gap, this paper proposes a Game-Theory-Integrated Modified Multi- Wireless Sensor Epidemic Malware Propagation (GTI-mSEMP) framework. This paper analyzed and compared the operational trajectories of Susceptible (S) and Recovered (R) node populations across three different operational regimes: Balanced Matchup, Exploit Surge and Hardened Defense. Numerical simulation results capture the real-time transient dynamics of the network state variables, demonstrating how the epidemic curve shifts when either the defensive or offensive scaling vectors hold an efficiency advantage. The proposed mathematical and numerical framework provides a rigorous foundation that can be deployed in highly adversarial network environments to evaluate dynamic malware propagation and predict localized node population states.

</details>


### [145] [Robust Harmful Features Under Jailbreak Attacks: Mechanistic Evidence from Attention Head Specialization in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28153)
*Yanchen Yin,Dongqi Han,Linghui Li*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 论文发现越狱攻击并非完全消除LLM的安全对齐，而是选择性抑制特定注意力头（ACHs），同时安全对齐头（SAHs）仍保持稳健激活，并据此提出无需训练的鲁棒检测方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 越狱攻击能够绕过LLM的安全对齐，但其内部机制尚未被充分理解。现有研究缺乏对攻击如何影响模型内部安全表征的细粒度分析。

Method: 通过注意力头级别的分析，识别出两类功能分化的注意力头：早期层的易受攻击头（ACHs）和中层的安全对齐头（SAHs）。通过消融实验验证其因果作用，并通过token级归因分析揭示攻击模板token对ACHs的抑制机制。

Result: 抑制少量ACHs即可在正常输入上诱导出类似越狱的行为；移除SAHs会削弱中层安全激活。攻击模板token是驱动ACH抑制的关键。基于SAHs持久激活的简单读取方法（无需训练）即可实现具有强对抗鲁棒性的检测性能。

Conclusion: 越狱攻击通过选择性抑制早期注意力头绕过拒绝决策，但中层的安全表征仍然保持稳健（即鲁棒有害特征）。利用这一鲁棒性，可以开发轻量级、无需训练的检测方法，有效对抗越狱攻击。

Abstract: Jailbreak attacks bypass LLM safety alignment, yet their mechanisms remain poorly understood. We provide evidence that attacks do not comprehensively eliminate safety features, but instead selectively suppress specific attention heads. We identify two functionally differentiated types: Adversarially Compromised Heads (ACHs) concentrated in early layers, which are suppressed under attacks, and Safety-Aligned Heads (SAHs) in mid-layers, which maintain robust activations even when attacks succeed. Ablation studies support the causal role of ACHs and the contribution of SAHs to robust activations: suppressing a small number of ACHs is sufficient to induce jailbreak-like behavior on normally refused inputs, while removing SAHs substantially weakens mid-layer safety activations. Token-level attribution further shows that ACH suppression is driven specifically by attack-template tokens, providing a mechanistic account of why attacks can bypass refusal decisions through ACH suppression while leaving internal safety signals sustained by SAHs -- a phenomenon we term Robust Harmful Features. To validate the practical significance of this robustness, we show that simply reading these persistent activations -- without any training -- yields competitive aggregate detection performance with strong adversarial robustness.

</details>

### [146] [Test-Input Generation for Tensor Programs: What Actually Finds Kernel Bugs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27396)
*Dipankar Sarkar*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 通过对26个算子（16个正确控制组和10个LLM风格错误变体）进行测试，发现仅边界形状采样在bug召回率（78%）和误报率（0%）之间取得最佳平衡，而对抗性值采样虽然召回率更高（99%）但误报率飙升至94%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 张量核的测试输入生成目前主要依赖经验性做法（民间传说），缺乏系统的量化评估和策略对比。

Method: 使用gpuemu操作模式感知的种子模糊测试器，在RTX 3060 GPU上对7种测试生成策略进行系统评估，通过变化形状候选集、数据类型组合和输入值分布，测量每种策略的bug召回率和控制组假阳性率。

Result: 边界形状采样以78%召回率和0%假阳性率成为安全最优策略；对抗性值采样召回率达99%但假阳性率高达94%；常规策略对softmax尾部掩码bug的召回率为0%，而边界策略分别提升至100%和62%。

Conclusion: 边界形状采样是操作上最安全的测试策略，不同策略对特定错误模式的捕获能力差异显著，强调了测试策略选择的重要性。

Abstract: Test-input generation for tensor kernels is folkloric. Most projects pick a representative shape and dtype, run a fixed-shape allclose-style check, and ship. We make the choices explicit and measure them. Using the gpuemu op-schema-aware seeded fuzzer (arXiv:2606.20128), we evaluate seven test-generation strategies across a 26-op corpus (16 correct controls and 10 LLM-style buggy variants seeded with documented transcription patterns) on an RTX 3060 GPU instance. Strategies vary the shape candidate set, the dtype mix, and the input value distribution. We report each strategy on two axes: bug recall and control false-positive (FP) rate. Boundary-only shape sampling is the operationally safe winner: 78% recall on the 10 buggy kernels with 0% FP on the 16 controls. Adversarial value sampling reaches higher recall (99%) but inflates control FP to 94% because the strategy injects NaN and Inf inputs and the validator's NaN check fires on every kernel that propagates them, not only on buggy kernels. On the two softmax tail-mask bugs the "regular" strategy (no boundary shapes) catches 0%, while boundary raises recall to 100% and 62% respectively. That gap is the clearest single signal in the data. The corpus result is about which seeded bug patterns each strategy catches, not about the bug rate of any specific deployed LLM.

</details>


### [147] [Implementing GenAI-Supported Learning in Software Engineering and Computer Science Education using Bloom's Taxonomy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27398)
*Vahid Garousi,Zafar Jafarov,Aytan Mövsümova,Leyla Memmedova,Hüseyn Mirzayev*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该研究设计了一个基于Bloom认知分类法的生成式AI使用框架，并在多门SE/CS课程中实施。研究发现，明确的认知层级指导能引导学生反思性地使用AI，学生认为AI对高阶认知活动（分析、评价、反思）最有价值，对基础学习帮助有限。研究结论认为，AI的教育价值在于学习目标、教学指导与学生自我调节之间的有意对齐。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式AI在软件工程教育中的使用带来了学习支持机会，同时也引发了对浅层学习和学术诚信的担忧。本研究旨在探索如何通过明确的教学指导（基于Bloom认知分类法）来支持负责任的GenAI使用，并了解学生和教师对GenAI辅助学习的看法。

Method: 研究者设计了一个Bloom对齐的GenAI框架，明确阐述了不同认知层级下GenAI的适当角色。该框架被嵌入到英国贝尔法斯特女王大学和阿塞拜疆技术大学多门SE/CS课程的课程说明、实验和评估中。通过匿名问卷和学习制品收集数据，以Bloom分类法作为分析视角进行主题分析。

Result: 学生认为GenAI对高阶认知活动（分析、评价、反思）最有价值，对基础学习不太适用。明确的Bloom层级指导促使学生反思性地使用AI，在需要独立思考时会有意延迟或选择不使用。学生和教师都报告了教学效益，同时也存在认知努力和教学设计工作量方面的挑战。

Conclusion: GenAI的教育价值在于认知学习目标、教学指导和学习者自我调节之间的有意对齐。Bloom分类法为SE/CS教育中负责任的GenAI使用提供了一个可扩展的、以教学法为导向的框架，是应对（而非禁止）AI使用的实用方案。

Abstract: Context: Generative AI adoption in software engineering education raises opportunities for learning support alongside concerns about superficial learning and academic integrity.
  Objective: This study investigates how explicit instructional guidance aligned with Bloom's taxonomy supports responsible GenAI use in SE/CS education, exploring student and instructor perceptions of GenAI-supported learning.
  Method: We designed a Bloom-aligned GenAI framework that articulated appropriate GenAI roles at different cognitive levels. The framework was embedded in course instructions, labs, and assessment across multiple SE/CS courses at Queen's University Belfast and Azerbaijan Technical University. Data were collected via anonymous questionnaires and learning artifacts, analyzed using thematic analysis with Bloom's taxonomy as an analytic lens.
  Results: Students perceived GenAI as most valuable for higher-order cognitive activities (analysis, evaluation, reflection) and less suitable for foundational learning. Explicit Bloom-level guidance influenced students to use GenAI reflectively, with delayed or intentional non-use when independent thinking was prioritized. Both students and instructors reported pedagogical benefits alongside challenges in cognitive effort and instructional design workload.
  Conclusion: GenAI's educational value lies in intentional alignment between cognitive learning goals, instructional guidance, and learner self-regulation. Bloom's taxonomy provides a scalable, pedagogy-driven framework for responsible GenAI use in SE/CS education, offering a practical alternative to enforcement-focused responses.

</details>


### [148] [Formal Grammars in Business Process Management: A Systematic Literature Review](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27399)
*Milliam Maxime Zekeng Ndadji*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文系统综述了34篇关于形式文法与业务流程管理（BPM）交叉领域的研究，识别出七个研究方向，并指出各方向并行发展、缺乏交叉综合，提出五个开放挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 形式文法在BPM中展现出生成、声明和分析能力，但该交叉领域的研究分散于不同方向，缺乏系统性梳理和综合，因此有必要进行文献综述以揭示现状和未来方向。

Method: 采用系统文献综述方法，筛选了34篇主要研究，识别出七个研究方向，并对每个方向的贡献、所用形式化方法和局限性进行了综合。

Result: 识别出七个研究流：过程文法、BWW框架下的建模语言文法、产生式规则文法、属性文法、图文法、文法推断和过程代数；发现这些方向在BPM全生命周期中均有应用，但缺乏交叉综合。

Conclusion: 形式文法已深刻影响BPM的各个阶段，但七个研究流并行发展。更深层、统一的文法理论利用有望推进BPM领域的发展，文中还提出了五个基于语料库的开放挑战。

Abstract: Business Process Management (BPM) is concerned with the systematic design, execution, monitoring, and improvement of business processes. Formal grammars have emerged as a particularly fruitful formalism for BPM, offering generative, declarative, and analytical capabilities that are uniquely well-suited to process-oriented concerns. This paper presents a systematic literature review of 34 primary studies at the intersection of formal grammars and BPM. We identify seven research streams: (i) process grammars for organizational process design; (ii) process modeling languages evaluated as grammars under the Bunge-Wand-Weber ontological framework; (iii) production-rule grammars for process structural specification and variant management; (iv) attribute grammars for the declarative specification and distributed execution of workflows; (v) graph grammars for the transformation, generation, and semantic analysis of process models; (vi) grammatical inference for process mining and discovery; and (vii) process algebras as grammar-like compositional frameworks for behavioral specification and verification. For each stream, we synthesize contributions, formalisms employed, and limitations. The review reveals that formal grammars have influenced BPM across every lifecycle phase (from organizational design to formal verification and data-driven discovery) yet the seven streams have developed largely in parallel, without cross-stream synthesis. We identify five corpus-grounded open challenges and argue that a deeper, unified exploitation of grammatical theory holds significant promise for advancing the state of the art in BPM.

</details>

Result: 发现现有模型在TB级代码集合上精度和可扩展性存在关键限制；提出的LLM方案能显著提升低性能模型的精度。

Benchmarking across multiple programming languages and datasets reveals critical limits in the precision and scalability of these models on Terabyte-scale source-code collections. TL;DR: 本文提出“软件世界模型”概念，评估AI模型对软件执行资源（峰值内存、运行时间、剖析器输出）的理解能力，发现前沿模型表现不佳，缺乏对软件执行过程的理解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码执行基准仅覆盖控制流，缺乏对执行资源（如内存、时间）等更广泛维度的评估，亟需更全面的测试来了解AI模型对软件执行的理解程度。

Method: 基于SWE-bench Verified数据，将评估维度从测试结果和异常类别扩展到峰值内存、墙钟时间、方法级和行级剖析器输出排名，测试多个AI模型（包括前沿模型）。

Result: 所有测试模型表现不佳，性能有限且行为不稳定，前沿模型同样如此。

Abstract: Software engineering, whether performed by humans or by AI agents, requires reasoning about how software behaves. We call the internal model that supports such reasoning the software world model, and view current code-execution benchmarks as covering one well-studied slice of it -- control flow. In this paper, we take a step toward a broader evaluation by shifting the observable axis to execution resources: alongside test outcome and exception class, we predict peak memory, wall-clock time, and ranked profiler outputs at method and line granularity. We use SWE-bench Verified as the source of data to hold the test close to real-world software engineering tasks. All tested models, frontier ones included, show modest performance and brittle behaviour, suggesting a notable lack of understanding of how software is executed, as opposed to how its source code is written.

### [151] [Speculative Refinement: A Hybrid Autoregressive Diffusion Decoding Strategy and Its Behavior Across Benchmarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27474)
*Aditi Gupta,Neel Mishra,Kushagra Trivedi,Pawan Kumar*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文通过SpecRef（一种结合自回归草稿与扩散精炼的混合生成方法）系统评估了多阶段生成系统，发现代码基准测试混淆了结构与逻辑正确性、精炼过程中存在"修正张力"现象、对数似然与生成评估产生不同模型排名、以及标准后处理对非自回归生成器失效等关键问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估方法无法有效衡量结合自回归解码与扩散解码的混合生成系统，需要更系统的评估框架来揭示多阶段生成管线的真实性能与潜在问题。

Method: 提出SpecRef方法（基于熵引导的掩码选择，用自回归草稿热启动掩码扩散语言模型），在6个基准（HumanEval、MBPP、GSM8K、BBH、ARC-Challenge、HellaSwag）上使用3种评估协议（执行pass@1、精确匹配、对数似然评分）进行系统评估。

Result: 发现了四个关键问题：代码基准将结构发现与逻辑正确性混为一谈；多阶段修正存在"修正张力"现象导致基线饱和天花板；对数似然与生成评估给出不同模型排名；标准Python后处理对非自回归生成器造成评估偏差。

Conclusion: 这些发现不仅限于SpecRef，对于任何多阶段或非自回归生成管线都具有普遍意义，指向更诊断性的评估实践需求。

Abstract: How should we evaluate generation systems that combine autoregressive (AR) and diffusion decoding? We study this question through Speculative Refinement (SpecRef), a training-free hybrid method that warm-starts a masked diffusion language model from an AR draft using entropy-guided selective masking. Evaluating SpecRef across six benchmarks (HumanEval, MBPP, GSM8K, BBH, ARC-Challenge, HellaSwag) with three distinct evaluation protocols (execution-based pass@1, exact-match, log-likelihood scoring), we surface several findings relevant beyond our specific system: (1) code benchmarks conflate structural discovery with logical correctness: providing a syntactic scaffold lifts accuracy from near zero to over 20% without changing the model, indicating that much of the baseline failure is structural; (2) a refinement tension phenomenon where multi-stage correction degrades already-correct tokens, exposing benchmark saturation ceilings invisible to single-model evaluation; (3) log-likelihood and generative evaluation produce different model rankings for the same model pair, suggesting they measure different capabilities; (4) standard Python post-processing silently breaks code evaluation for non-AR generators. These observations apply to any multi-stage or non-autoregressive generation pipeline and point toward more diagnostic evaluation practices.

</details>


### [152] [Contextual Associations Between Webpage Elements for Web Accessibility: An Empirical Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27506)
*Kishan Rakesh,Shiyi Wei*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本研究探索能否通过链接预测从无障碍树中恢复网页元素间人类感知的上下文关联，并评估其跨网站泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 屏幕阅读器用户在按元素列表导航网页时，常遇到如"Read more"这类符合W3C规范但在孤立状态下无法理解的易访问名称。周围的元素本可用于解释这些名称，但缺乏机制将它们连接到目标元素。目前尚无实证研究探讨如何选择与目标相关的上下文元素。

Method: 将在35个网站上构建人类标注的上下文关联数据集（每页3名独立标注者），将页面表示为从无障碍树衍生出的图，并增强DOM和CSS的空间与语义特征。比较四种机器学习模型（MLP、GCN、GAT、SEAL）与两种启发式基线，采用留一站点交叉验证和预注册统计框架，使用Hit@K和MRR评估。

Result: 在5个站点的作者标注试点研究中，四种学习模型的Hit@10范围为0.16-0.85，两种启发式基线为0.08-0.30。最终结果将在完成计划实验后报告。

Conclusion: 本研究贡献了网页上下文关联的人类标注数据集、链接预测用于无障碍树图上下文选择的实证评估，以及跨网站泛化分析。

Abstract: [Context] Screen reader users navigating webpages by element list often encounter accessible names such as "Read more" that are valid under the W3C Accessible Name and Description Computation specification but uninterpretable in isolation. The surrounding elements that would make these names meaningful exist in the page but are not linked to the target by any mechanism. No prior work has empirically studied how to select which surrounding elements are contextually relevant to a given target. [Objective] This registered report investigates whether human-perceived contextual associations between webpage elements can be recovered from the accessibility tree using link prediction, and whether the learned associations generalize across websites. [Method] We will construct a dataset of human-annotated contextual associations on 35 websites, stratified across the Tranco top-million list, with three independent annotators per page. Each page is represented as a graph derived from its accessibility tree, augmented with spatial and semantic features from the DOM and CSS. We compare four machine learning models (MLP, GCN, GAT, and SEAL) against two heuristic baselines under leave-one-site-out cross-validation with a pre-registered statistical framework, using Hit@K and MRR. [Results] We have conducted a five-site author-annotated pilot study to establish the pipelines and parameterize the power simulation, with pilot Hit@10 ranging from 0.16 to 0.85 across four learned models and 0.08 to 0.30 across two heuristic baselines. The final results will be reported after the planned experiments and analyses are completed. [Conclusion] The study contributes a human-annotated dataset of contextual associations on webpages, an empirical evaluation of link prediction for context selection on accessibility-tree graphs, and a cross-site generalization analysis.

</details>


### [153] [Test Case Selection for Deep Neural Networks: A Replication Study on LLMs for Code](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27601)
*Ali Asgari,Mitchell Olsthoorn,Annibale Panichella*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文对深度神经网络中的测试用例选择（TCS）技术进行了大规模复制研究，将其推广到LLM代码模型。在3个代码分类任务上评估了13种选择策略，发现只有部分视觉DNN的结论适用于LLM代码模型，其中不确定性特征对早期故障发现有效，表示特征对精度估计更鲁棒，且效果因任务和模型而异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的TCS技术研究主要聚焦于视觉DNN，其在LLM代码模型上的泛化能力尚不明确，需要系统性的复制研究来验证。

Method: 在克隆检测、漏洞检测和技术债务预测三个代码分类任务上，对17个微调模型实例、7种预测特征和13种选择策略（包括12种特征感知策略和随机采样基线）进行系统评估。

Result: 只有部分视觉DNN的发现可推广到LLM代码模型；不确定性特征在早期故障发现上表现良好，表示特征在精度估计上更鲁棒；效果在不同任务和模型间存在显著差异。

Conclusion: TCS技术在LLM代码模型上的有效性具有上下文依赖性，本研究为超越视觉DNN的TCS可复制性提供了实证依据。

Abstract: Recently, test case selection (TCS) techniques have been explored to support the operational evaluation of deep neural networks (DNNs) under limited testing budgets, where labeling cost is a primary concern and uncovering model failures early is a key objective. Although prior studies report promising results, existing empirical evaluations focus almost exclusively on vision-based DNNs and datasets, leaving it unclear whether prior findings generalize to LLM code models. This paper presents a large-scale replication study of TCS techniques in the context of LLM code models. We re-examine established TCS strategies originally proposed for DNNs and complement them with statistical sampling strategies not previously evaluated for TCS. We assess their effectiveness on three code-related classification tasks: clone detection, vulnerability detection, and technical debt prediction. The study spans 17 task-specific fine-tuned model instances, 7 predictive features, and 13 selection strategies, including 12 feature-aware strategies and simple random sampling (SRS) as a feature-agnostic baseline. We evaluate performance along two dimensions: accuracy estimation and early failure discovery. The results indicate that only a subset of findings reported for vision-based DNNs generalize when TCS is applied to LLMs for code. In particular, uncertainty-based features are effective for early failure discovery, while representation-based features are more robust for accuracy estimation. At the same time, performance varies substantially across tasks and models, indicating that TCS effectiveness is context-dependent. Overall, this study provides empirical evidence on the replicability of TCS techniques beyond vision-based deep learning and offers insights into their use for the operational evaluation of LLMs for code.

### [154] [LLM-Assisted Model-Based GUI Testing for Vue.js Web Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27665)
*Tao Li,Chenhui Cui,Rubing Huang,Dave Towey,Shikai Guo,Lei Ma*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出LLMVue框架，利用大语言模型从Vue.js源码自动生成可执行页面转换图（PTG），实现基于模型的GUI测试，在10个开源项目上验证了高精度、高召回率和更好的测试覆盖率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Vue.js应用日益复杂，需要自动化测试保障可靠性，但基于模型的GUI测试在Vue.js上难以应用，因为转换候选分布在路由配置和单文件组件中，需要具体化并规范化为可执行的页面转换图。

Method: 提出LLMVue框架，利用大语言模型（GPT-4o）从Vue.js源码中推断组件层次结构和路由转换，合并多个单文件组件形成统一的页面转换图（PTG），并基于该图进行模型驱动的GUI测试。

Result: 在10个开源Vue.js项目上评估，生成的PTG具有高精确率和高召回率、低图编辑距离；相比随机探索基线，LLMVue引导的测试在相同时间约束下显著提升了覆盖率和探索效率。

Conclusion: 首次将大语言模型用于Vue.js应用的基于模型的GUI测试，通过源码级PTG提取实现了有效的自动化测试，验证了LLM在模型生成方面的潜力。

Abstract: Vue.js is a popular framework for building modern web applications. As Vue.js functionality and tooling support grow, ensuring its reliability (through automated testing) is becoming increasingly important. Although model-based testing has been successfully used to automate graphical user interface (GUI) testing on other platforms, its application to Vue.js remains challenging: Transition candidates, which are spread across router configurations and single-file components (SFCs), must be concretized and normalized into an executable page transition graph (PTG) for testing. To address this, we propose the LLMVue framework, which uses a large language model (LLM) to generate a PTG from Vue.js source code. LLMVue infers component hierarchies and route transitions, merging them into a unified PTG across multiple SFCs. We evaluated LLMVue on a collection of ten open-source Vue.js projects from GitHub, using GPT-4o as the LLM backbone. The constructed graphs demonstrate high precision and recall, with low graph edit distance. LLMVue -guided testing also significantly improves the coverage and exploration efficiency, compared to a random exploration baseline (with the same time constraints). To the best of our knowledge, this is the first use of LLMs for model-based GUI testing of Vue.js applications using source-level PTG extraction.

### [155] [BashCoder-R1: Towards Robust and Explainable Bash Code Generation with Robustness-Aware Group Relative Policy Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27733)
*Lei Yu,Peng Wang,Jia Xu,Jingyuan Zhang,Xin Wang,Jiajia Ma,Li Yang,Changzhi Deng,Zenghua Wang,Fengjun Zhang*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 提出BashCoder-R1框架，通过持续预训练、长思维链监督微调和鲁棒性强化学习，在Bash脚本生成任务中实现高语法正确率、低鲁棒性警告率，并在新基准BashBench上显著超越DeepSeek-V3.2等基线模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM生成的Bash脚本存在两大问题：不可审计的"黑箱"推理过程，以及生成的代码存在严重鲁棒性漏洞。这两个问题相互关联，亟需同时解决。

Method: 提出三阶段流水线：(1) 持续预训练(CPT)使模型适应Bash范式；(2) 长思维链监督微调(L-CoT SFT)在专家验证的推理-代码样本上训练；(3) 鲁棒性感知的组相对策略优化(R-GRPO)，通过加权奖励优化语法正确性、鲁棒性(shellcheck)和格式正确性。

Result: 在BashBench基准(952个任务)上，单行/多行任务SyntaxPass达100.00%/94.97%，RobustPass达95.99%/79.33%，FullRate达90.04%/73.18%，比最强基线DeepSeek-V3.2分别高出37.82%和20.18%。

Conclusion: BashCoder-R1在功能、鲁棒性和清晰度三个维度上均达到最高质量评分，有效解决了Bash脚本生成中的可解释性和鲁棒性问题。

Abstract: Bash scripts are the cornerstone of system administration and DevOps automation, where code quality directly impacts system stability and security. In automated Bash script generation using Large Language Models (LLMs), two interconnected failures emerge: unauditable "black box" reasoning and critical robustness vulnerabilities in generated code. To address both, we propose BashCoder-R1, a novel framework for robust and explainable Bash script generation. Our pipeline combines: (1) Continual Pre-training (CPT) to specialize the model on Bash paradigms; (2) Long Chain-of-Thought Supervised Fine-Tuning (L-CoT SFT) on expert-validated reasoning-and-code samples to emulate proactive risk-aware thinking; and (3) Robustness-Aware Group Relative Policy Optimization (R-GRPO), a reinforcement learning phase optimizing a weighted reward for syntax correctness, robustness (via shellcheck), and format correctness. We evaluate on BashBench, a new benchmark of 952 real-world tasks (773 single-line, 179 multi-line). BashCoder-R1 achieves SyntaxPass (100.00%/94.97%), RobustWarnRate (4.01%/16.47%), RobustPass (95.99%/79.33%), FuncRate (93.01%/93.85%), and FullRate (90.04%/73.18%) for single-line/multi-line tasks, outperforming the strongest baseline DeepSeek-V3.2 (Reasoning) by 37.82% and 20.18% in FullRate. Human evaluation on Functionality, Robustness, and Clarity further confirms BashCoder-R1 achieves the highest quality ratings.

### [156] [UNICS: Multilingual Code Search via Unified Pseudocode and Contrastive Transfer Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27747)
*Ye Fan,Jidong Ge,Chuanyi Li,Liguo Huang,Bin Luo*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: UNICS是一个两阶段训练的多语言代码搜索框架，通过伪代码统一表示和语义切片策略，在跨语言代码搜索任务上达到SOTA性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有预训练模型在多语言代码搜索中存在数据不平衡、跨语言语义干扰、统一表示（如AST/IR）信息丢失等问题，且对比学习策略忽略了对困难正样本的挖掘。

Method: 两阶段训练策略：第一阶段使用伪代码作为统一表示进行预训练，学习跨语言算法级逻辑；第二阶段采用多任务迁移学习，将代码分解为语义切片（如API调用、函数体），并引入困难正样本挖掘和跨语言动态困难负样本采样任务。

Result: 在多个多语言和跨语言基准测试上达到SOTA性能，尤其在低资源语言的零样本迁移任务中表现出优越的泛化能力和性能平衡。

Abstract: While pre-trained models have achieved remarkable success in code search, their multilingual capabilities remain a major hurdle, plagued by data imbalance, cross-lingual semantic interference, and the loss of critical information from existing unified representations like Abstract Syntax Trees (ASTs) or Intermediate Representations (IRs). Furthermore, conventional contrastive learning strategies often rely on simplistic hard negative sampling while overlooking the potential of mining hard positives to learn code's intrinsic semantic invariance. To address these challenges, we introduce UNICS, a framework for multilingual code search built on a two-stage training strategy. In the first stage, UNICS is pre-trained on a novel dataset we constructed, which uses pseudo-code as a unified representation to learn a cross-lingual, algorithm-level logic that preserves full semantic fidelity. The second stage employs a multi-task transfer learning strategy that adapts this general knowledge to specific languages by decomposing code into semantic slices (e.g., API calls, function bodies) and incorporating tasks for hard positive mining and cross-lingual dynamic hard negative sampling. Experimental results demonstrate that UNICS achieves state-of-the-art performance across multiple multilingual and cross-lingual benchmarks, showcasing superior generalization and performance balance, especially in zero-shot transfer tasks to low-resource languages.

### [158] [Evolution-Aware Regression Test Prioritization of ML-Enabled Systems Using Gradient-Based Behavior Vectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28037)
*Eunho Cho,Donghwan Shin,In-Young Ko*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 提出GBV-PD方法，利用梯度行为向量空间实现演化感知的回归测试优先级排序，无需运行演化模型即可预测测试用例损失变化方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ML组件的演化（重训练、微调等）使已有测试结果失效，需要高效的回归测试优先级排序方法，且需考虑性能变化的<方向性>。

Method: 将每个测试用例表示为其在原始模型下损失梯度的低维投影（GBV），再将演化模型的参数更新投影到同一PCA基上，通过对齐程度估计损失增减方向，无需运行演化模型。

Result: 在分类和回归任务中，GBV-PD持续优于非方向性基线，与全梯度参考方法相当，且通过GBV缓存实现了更好的时间和存储效率。

Conclusion: 行为空间思想可以落地为实用高效的回归测试机制，支持ML系统的持续演化场景。

Abstract: The machine learning(ML) component of an ML-enabled system evolves through retraining, fine-tuning, and optimization, so previously valid test results may no longer hold. A single evolution step can worsen performance on some test cases while improving others, making regression test prioritization inherently directional. We present Gradient-based Behavior Vector-Parameter Delta(GBV-PD), the first approach to operationalize the behavior vector space for evolution-aware regression test prioritization. GBV-PD represents each test case as a gradient-based vector(GBV), a low-dimensional projection of its loss gradient under the original model. It then projects the observed parameter update of the evolved model onto the same PCA basis and uses the resulting alignment to estimate whether each test case's loss is likely to increase or decrease, without running the evolved model on test cases during prioritization. In an empirical study across classification and regression tasks, GBV-PD consistently outperformed non-directional baselines and remained competitive with a full-gradient reference, while offering better time and storage profiles for repeated updates via reusable GBV caching. These results show that behavior-space ideas can be operationalized into a practical and efficient mechanism for repeated-update regression testing of evolving ML-enabled systems.

</details>

However, significant gaps between source and binary representations, including function inlining, create challenges in cross-domain function detection. Existing approaches primarily rely on string literals or structural similarities between entire functions, failing to capture detailed code behavior and generating many false alarms. SBridge addresses these limitations through a key innovation: control block-based function matching, which encapsulates essential functional features by segmenting functions into meaningful units such as conditionals and loops. Leveraging control blocks as a cross-domain representation, SBridge enables precise measurement of function similarity between source and binary code, effectively overcoming challenges posed by function inlining and stripped binaries. For evaluation, we collected 3,904 real-world C/C++ binaries from BinKit. In experiments identifying binary functions identical to input source functions, despite approximately 40% of binary functions being inlined, SBridge achieved 75.13% recall@1 and 80.98% recall@5, outperforming existing approaches, which achieved up to 43.31% recall@1 and 50.2% recall@

Motivation: 现有编译器测试技术仅关注单语言编译，但现代JVM应用常集成多种编程语言，跨语言编译中的语义差异可能导致严重误编译错误，缺乏针对跨语言编译的测试方法。

Method: 利用Kotlin编译器的统一中间表示(IR)合成跨语言测试程序，并应用七种变异算子增加测试程序多样性，实现差分测试框架。

Result: 在五个主流JVM编译器最新版本上发现32个已确认bug：Kotlin 15个、Groovy 4个、Scala 3有7个、Scala 2有2个、Java 4个。

Conclusion: CrossLangFuzzer能有效发现跨语言JVM编译中的缺陷，填补了跨语言编译器测试的空白，工具已开源。

Abstract: Modern JVM software increasingly integrates multiple programming languages, such as Java, Kotlin, Groovy, and Scala, within a single application. Supporting such interoperability requires JVM compilers to perform cross-language compilation while reconciling subtle semantic differences across language boundaries. Errors in this process can lead to critical miscompilations, yet existing compiler testing techniques focus exclusively on isolated, singlelanguage compilation. To address this gap, we present CrossLangFuzzer, the first differential testing framework for cross-language JVM compilation. CrossLangFuzzer leverages the Kotlin compiler's unified intermediate representation (IR) to synthesize cross-language test programs. It further applies seven mutation operators to diversify generated test programs and improve bug-finding capability. Evaluated on the latest versions of five major JVM compilers, CrossLangFuzzer uncovered 32 confirmed bugs, including 15 in Kotlin, 4 in Groovy, 7 in Scala 3, 2 in Scala 2, and 4 in Java. CrossLangFuzzer is open-source at https://github.com/XYZboom/CrossLangFuzzer

</details>


### [163] [Humanizing Automatically Generated Unit Test Suites with LLM-Based Refactoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28229)
*Wendkûuni C. Ouédraogo,Yinghua Li,Xueqi Dang,Paweł Borsukiewicz,Lingfeng Bao,Anil Koyuncu,Jacques Klein,David Lo,Tegawendé F. Bissyandé*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 提出TestHumanizer混合方法，将SBST生成的编译测试套件通过LLM进行受控重构，在保持编译有效性和覆盖率的同时提升可读性和可维护性，在31,500次重构中达到88-98%编译率，开发者研究表明可读性和采用意愿显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SBST生成的测试套件虽然编译率高、覆盖好，但可读性和可维护性差；LLM虽能生成更自然的测试，但直接生成编译率仅51-78%。如何结合两者优势是一个亟待解决的问题。

Method: 提出TestHumanizer混合方法：先用SBST(EvoSuite)生成可编译的测试套件，再将LLM作为受控重构层，在保持行为不变、编译有效的前提下，优化命名、结构和开发者导向的清晰度。在Defects4J和SF110的350个类上，用gpt-4o和mistral-large-2407在三种上下文配置下进行31,500次重构实验。

Result: 编译率达88-98%，接近EvoSuite的100%基线；结构覆盖率基本保持（偏差1-2个百分点）；86-95%重构满足忠实重构阈值；可读性、控制流复杂度、认知复杂度和结构坏味道均有改善；基于摘要的设置效果最优；开发者研究（30类、444个方法）显示可读性和采用意愿显著提升（Wilcoxon p<0.01）。

Conclusion: LLM最有效的角色不是独立生成器，而是作为验证门控的精化层，增强稳健的SBST输出。基于摘要的上下文设置提供了最佳的鲁棒性平衡。

Abstract: Search-based test generation tools such as EvoSuite produce compilable and high-coverage unit tests at scale, but their suites are often hard to read and maintain. LLMs can generate more natural tests, yet direct generation remains brittle, with compilation rates of only 51-78% in our study. We introduce TestHumanizer, a hybrid SBST+LLM approach that uses LLMs as controlled refactoring layers over compilable SBST suites to improve naming, structure, and developer-oriented clarity while preserving behavior and compilation validity. We evaluate TestHumanizer on 350 classes from Defects4J and SF110. EvoSuite generates 15 suites per class, and each suite is refactored under three context configurations using gpt-4o and mistral-large-2407, yielding 31,500 refactorings. TestHumanizer reaches 88-98% compilation rates, close to EvoSuite's 100% baseline and clearly above direct LLM generation. Structural coverage is largely preserved, typically within 1-2 percentage points, and 86-95% of refactorings satisfy a composite faithful-refactoring threshold. Refactored suites also improve predicted readability, reduce control-flow and cognitive complexity, and mitigate structural smells. The summary-based setting offers the most robust trade-off, while long code-centric prompts are more prone to hallucination-induced failures. A developer study on 30 classes and 444 test methods confirms significant gains in perceived readability and willingness to adopt, with Wilcoxon p less than 0.01 and substantial inter-rater agreement. Overall, LLMs are most effective not as standalone generators but as validation-gated refinement layers over robust SBST outputs.

</details>


### [164] [Govern the Repository, Not the Agent: Measuring Ecosystem-Level Risk in AI-Native Software](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28235)
*Daniel Russo*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 研究发现，AI智能体在代码仓库中的集成摩擦（integration friction）约有50%归因于仓库本身而非单一贡献者。智能体贡献导致的仓库级摩擦（组内相关系数0.30）是人类贡献（0.16）的近两倍，这种差异在控制多种因素后依然显著。结论是AI原生软件应基于生态系统层面而非单个智能体进行衡量和治理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估方式孤立地衡量单个智能体在基准测试上的表现，忽略了多个智能体同时修改共享仓库时产生的累积问题。作者质疑这种“单个组件”的评估范式是否合理。

Method: 分析了超过93万个智能体发起的PR，测量集成摩擦的变化中有多少可归因于仓库本身（而非贡献者、大小、智能体等因素），并对比智能体与人类贡献在仓库级摩擦上的差异。

Result: 约一半的集成摩擦变化由仓库本身解释；智能体贡献的仓库级摩擦（ICC=0.30）是人类（ICC=0.16）的近两倍，且该差距在控制代码库大小、年龄、任务形态、流程成熟度和合并路径后依然存在。

Conclusion: 集成摩擦的风险是生态系统属性，而非单个智能体属性。AI原生软件的评估和治理应从单一智能体层面转向生态系统层面。

Abstract: Autonomous coding agents now open and merge pull requests in shared repositories at scale, and the field evaluates them the way it has always evaluated components, one agent at a time, on isolated benchmark tasks. Yet agents that each pass their own tests still leave repositories that accumulate problems no single contribution accounts for. We ask whether this problem belongs to the individual agent or to the repository where it accumulates. We study integration friction, the cost of integrating a contribution into a codebase that other contributors are concurrently changing. Across more than 930,000 agent-authored pull requests, we measure how much of the variation in friction stays with the repository after the contribution, its author, its size, and its agent are accounted for. About half does, and it survives full controls. In the same repositories, agent-authored contributions concentrate this repository-level friction roughly twice as much as human ones (intraclass correlation 0.30 versus 0.16), a gap that holds after controlling for codebase size, age, task shape, process maturity, and merge path. The risk is a property of the ecosystem, not the agent. AI-native software is therefore better measured and governed at the ecosystem level than one agent at a time.

</details>

### [165] [AI-Model Network: Concept, Current State and Future](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27382)
*Li Zhetao,Zeng Xiyu,Wang Jianhui,Xiao Yong,Liu Zhongren,Wu Junru,Lai Junjie,Huang Jijun,Long Saiqin*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文受互联网发展启发，提出世界人工智能模型网络（AI-ModelNet）的概念、愿景与系统架构，旨在通过建立模型间通路实现异构大模型的互联互通、能力共享与协同推理，以解决当前大模型训练成本高、部署复杂及模型协作瓶颈等问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大模型实际应用受限于高昂训练成本和部署复杂性，正转向轻量级、私有化与领域专用模型。随着异构模型数量激增，如何实现模型间有效交互与协作成为亟待解决的关键瓶颈。

Method: 借鉴互联网发展经验，提出AI-ModelNet范式，包括其系统愿景与分层架构；通过原型系统和多样化应用案例验证框架可行性。

Result: 提出了AI-ModelNet的概念与层次化架构，并通过原型系统和应用案例初步验证了该框架的可行性。

Conclusion: AI-ModelNet为异构大模型间的互联互通与协同推理提供了新范式，未来研究方向值得进一步探索。

Abstract: While the primary function of computers lies in computation and processing, the core value of the Internet is rooted in sharing and collaboration. Computers create the Internet, and the Internet empowers the value of computers. The rapid development of the Internet, cloud computing, and big data is pushing artificial intelligence into the era of large models (LMs). However, the practical application of LMs is currently hindered by high training costs and deployment complexities, driving a shift toward lightweight, private, and domain-specific models. With the rapid proliferation and wide distribution of heterogeneous models, enabling effective interaction and collaboration among them has emerged as a critical bottleneck that urgently needs to be addressed in LM development. Drawing inspiration from the development of the Internet, this paper proposes the concept, vision, and system architecture of world wide AI-model network (AI-ModelNet). It is a novel paradigm that achieves interconnection, capability sharing, and collaborative reasoning by establishing pathways between models. We first briefly review the current state of single-model and multi-model research. Subsequently, the systemic vision and hierarchical architecture of AI-ModelNet are articulated, followed by validation of the framework's feasibility through a prototype system and diverse application cases. Finally, key directions for future research are discussed preliminarily.

</details>


### [166] [When Does Personality Composition Matter for Multi-Agent LLM Teams?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27443)
*Aryan Keluskar,Amrita Bhattacharjee,Huan Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究通过操纵大语言模型的个性特质（宜人性），在编码、开放协作和竞争谈判三个任务领域考察了多智能体团队表现。结果发现，个性影响严重依赖于任务结构：编码任务中低宜人性虽改变沟通风格但不影响任务完成；而在开放协作和谈判任务中则显著降低表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往研究仅关注个性提示如何改变LLM的沟通风格（如低宜人性产生对抗性语言，高宜人性产生合作性语言），但沟通风格与任务表现之间的关系尚未在多领域得到系统检验。

Method: 在三种任务领域（结构化编码、开放研究协作、竞争谈判）中，对前沿LLM多智能体团队的宜人性特质进行操纵，观察其对团队表现的影响。

Result: 个性效应严重依赖于任务结构：编码任务中低宜人性引发巨大沟通风格转变，但对里程碑完成影响甚微；在开放协作和谈判任务中，同样的操纵显著降低表现。

Conclusion: 讨论了多智能体系统设计的启示以及个性操纵的局限性。

Abstract: Personality prompting shapes how large language models communicate, yet whether these behavioral shifts affect objective task outcomes remains under-explored. Prior work shows that agents prompted with low agreeableness produce adversarial language, while those prompted with high agreeableness become cooperative, but the relationship between communication style and task performance has not been systematically examined across multiple domains. In this work, we investigate whether personality composition matters for multi-agent team performance by manipulating personality traits across frontier LLMs on three task domains: structured coding, open-ended research collaboration, and competitive bargaining. We find that personality effects depend critically on task structure. In coding tasks, low agreeableness leads to large communication shifts that have little effect on milestone completion. In open-ended collaboration and bargaining, the same manipulation substantially degrades performance. We discuss implications for multi-agent system design and the limits of personality manipulation.

</details>


### [167] [Internalizing the Future: A Unified Agentic Training Paradigm for World Model Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27483)
*Xuan Zhang,Zhijian Zhou,Lingfeng Qiao,Yulei Qin,Ke Li,Xing Sun,Xiaoyu Tan,Chao Qu,Yuan Qi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种三阶段训练范式，使LLM智能体具备内部世界模型能力，实现前瞻性规划和基于条件的成功估计（Q值的文本类比），从而在长周期任务中超越传统反应式智能体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准LLM智能体在长周期任务中本质上是反应式的，缺乏人类那种“what-if”推理能力，无法在行动前模拟未来结果，导致规划效果受限。

Method: 提出三阶段训练范式：(i) World Model Agentic Mid-Training (WM-AMT) 注入潜在预测能力；(ii) Format-Eliciting SFT (FE-SFT) 结构化该能力；(iii) Foresight-Conditioned Reinforcement Learning (FC-RL) 优化生成模拟的校准性和实用性。

Result: 在搜索和数学推理任务上，该方法持续优于其他训练基线，表明能力优先的训练流程能实现有基础且校准的前瞻性。

Conclusion: 有效的内部世界建模需要能力优先的训练流程，仅仅在post-training中微调前瞻性轨迹会导致表面模仿，缺乏真正的预测基础。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents have demonstrated strong capability in sequential decision-making, yet they remains fundamentally reactive in long-horizon tasks. Unlike humans who employ "what-if" reasoning to evaluate potential plans before commitment, standard agents lack an internal world model to simulate future outcomes. Therefore, we propose to internalize future-aware planning by training a single autoregressive model to verbalize both a prospective state rollout and a plan-conditioned success estimate-a textual analogue of the Q-value. Crucially, we identify a format-capability gap: simply fine-tuning agents on look-ahead traces during post-training leads to superficial mimicry of foresight without genuine predictive grounding. To bridge this gap, we introduce a three-stage training paradigm: (i) World Model Agentic Mid-Training (WM-AMT) to inject latent predictive capabilities into the policy; (ii) Format-Eliciting SFT (FE-SFT) to structure this injected capability; and (iii) Foresight-Conditioned Reinforcement Learning (FC-RL) to refine the calibration and utility of the generated simulations. Evaluated on search and mathematical reasoning tasks, our approach consistently outperforms other training baselines. Our results demonstrate that effective internal world modeling in LLM agents requires a capability-first training pipeline to achieve grounded and calibrated foresight.

</details>


### [168] [Odyssey: Constructing Verifiable Local Truth-Preserving Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27593)
*Sridhar Mahadevan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出ODYSSEY——一个基于层论（sheaf theory）的范畴论框架，用于构建可验证、保持局部真理的基础模型，通过"铸厂"（foundries）作为建筑块组件，支持局部上下文覆盖、表示族、限制映射、胶合规则、阻塞策略、更新义务和人机协作视图。通用铸厂学习（UFL）通过左、右Kan扩展形式化铸厂构建，Foundry SQL（FSQL）提供类型化查询接口，TICKET认证机制实现外部模型准入。该框架在多种铸厂上实现并测试，将在ICML 2026以2.5小时教程形式呈现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基础模型缺乏形式化的局部真理保持机制和可验证性，不同知识域（证据推理、决策、金融、科学等）缺乏统一的构建范式，难以实现异构知识的可靠组合与审计。

Method: 采用范畴论中的层论和Kan扩展作为核心数学工具：左Kan扩展将局部构件滚动为候选铸厂，右Kan扩展强制执行限制、胶合、阻塞和论证条件；引入TICKET（基于因果Kan扩展变换器的拓扑斯集成）认证机制；设计FSQL类型化查询语言访问铸厂工件。

Result: 在证据/论证、操作决策、制度/金融、市场含义、科学挑战、研究计划、助手构建和评估框架等多种铸厂上完成实现与测试，支持领域构建、工件重放、层诊断、扎根Toulmin论证/局部LLM审查、残差阻塞账本和因果声明提取等功能。

Conclusion: ODYSSEY证明了同一套范畴论机制能够统一支持多种异构知识域的构建与验证，为构建可审计、可解释的基础模型提供了理论框架和工程实现。

Abstract: We introduce a categorical framework called ODYSSEY for constructing verifiable, local truth-preserving foundation models as compositions of foundries: building-block architectural components that specify a cover of local contexts, local representation families, restriction maps, gluing rules, obstruction policies, update obligations, and human-facing views. A foundry is an organized sheaf of knowledge that carries within it an argumentation component. Concrete foundries are built from generic foundries such as evidence/argument, operational decision, institutional/financial, market meaning, scientific challenge, research-program, assistant-build, and evaluation-harness foundries. Universal Foundry Learning (UFL) formalizes foundry construction as a composition of left and right Kan extensions, with left Kan extension rolling local artifacts into candidate foundries and right Kan extension enforcing the restriction, gluing, obstruction, and argumentation conditions required for promotion. Foundry SQL (FSQL) is a small typed query surface for slicing maintained foundry artifacts that uses TICKET (Topos Integration using Causal Kan Extension Transformers) certification for admitting external or pre-built models into durable ODYSSEY state. ODYSSEY is fully implemented and tested across a wide spectrum of concrete foundries, showing that the same categorical machinery supports domain construction, artifact replay, sheaf diagnostics, grounded Toulmin/local-LLM scrutiny, residual-obstruction ledgers, and optimized TICKET-compatible causal-claim extraction across heterogeneous sources. This paper is to be presented as a 2.5 hour tutorial at ICML 2026. The tutorial home page is at https://bit.ly/4ajS0nA.

</details>


### [169] [DysLexLens: A Low-Resource LLM Framework for Analysing Dyslexic Learners Insights from Online Forums](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27619)
*Dana Rezazadegan,Atie Kia,Phongpadid Nandavong,Dominique Carlon,Jeremy Nguyen,Abhik Banerjee,James Marshall,Anthony McCosker,Yong-Bin Kang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出DysLexLens，一个利用低资源LLM框架分析阅读障碍学习者AI使用经验的工具，通过Reddit论坛数据实现端到端的证据可追溯分析，并验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 阅读障碍学习者越来越多地使用AI工具，但其真实使用体验尚未被充分研究，缺乏针对性的分析方法。

Method: 构建DysLexLens框架：字典驱动过滤构建语料库、知识图谱（KG）问题推理、可验证查询生成、定量（RAGAS和查询鲁棒性）与人工评估相结合。

Result: 在Reddit论坛数据上使用30个问题验证了DysLexLens的有效性，并展示了对其他低资源论坛数据的潜在泛化能力。

Conclusion: DysLexLens为分析阅读障碍学习者的AI使用体验提供了有效的端到端框架，且具备可复现性和泛化潜力。

Abstract: Dyslexic learners increasingly use artificial intelligence (AI) tools to support reading, writing, organisation, and study-related tasks. However, their lived experiences with these tools remain largely underexamined. This paper proposes DysLexLens, a low-resource LLM framework, designed to analyse dyslexic learners experience with AI through online forum discussions. DysLexLens is designed as an end-to-end, evidence-traceable architecture which transforms noisy social media posts into a dictionary-driven corpora, provides knowledge-graph (KG)-based question reasoning, generates verifiable query responses, and enables response evaluation through quantitative and human-grounded assessment. DysLexLens has four key features. First, it employs a dictionary-driven filtering method to construct a more focused Reddit corpus on dyslexia and AI, filtering out noisy and weakly related posts to improve the relevance of data collected from low-resource forum contexts. Second, it integrates LLM-assisted semantic analysis with KG-based query reasoning to uncover meaningful patterns. Third, it has quantitative evaluation metrics (RAGAS and Query Robustness) to measure LLM-generated response performance. Fourth, it provides structured qualitative validation guidelines for assessing response quality, with a specific focus on hallucination and evidence alignment. We demonstrate the effectiveness of DysLexLens using dyslexia-related Reddit forum data and 30 questions. The results show its potential generalisability to other low-resource forum data contexts. DysLexLens, sample data, questions and evaluation results are available at Github to support reproducibility.

</details>


### [170] [MER-R1: Multimodal Emotion Reasoning via Slow-Fast Thinking Synergy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27652)
*Zhiyuan Han,Beier Zhu,Wenwen Tong,Chengwei Qin,Xinyi Wang,Jiayu Zhang,Jiangnan Chen,Hewei Guo,Dongchuan Ran,Lewei Lu,Xun Yang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出MER-R1框架，通过强化学习将慢思考（精准）与快思考（高召回）的互补性进行显式优化，实现多模态情感识别中推理过程既提升可解释性又带来准确率提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究表明，显式推理虽提升可解释性，但未必带来更好的多模态情感识别准确率。作者希望解决慢思考与快思考之间的权衡问题，让推理真正有益于情感识别。

Method: 提出MER-R1框架，包含：(1) 双目标解耦，将召回率和精确度分离为两个优化信号进行联合优化；(2) 慢-快置信度校准，将最终慢思考答案与快思考直觉对齐；(3) 理论证明该协同机制能减轻优化过程中的方差干扰。

Result: 在MER-UniBench和MME-Emotion基准上取得最先进性能，证明推理能够真正有益于情感识别。

Conclusion: 快思考偏向高召回（更广泛、更自信的预测），慢思考偏向高精确度（保守过滤错误类别）。通过MER-R1框架将两者互补性转化为显式优化，实现了慢快思考的统一，使推理既增强可解释性又提升识别准确率。

Abstract: We find that explicit reasoning does not necessarily translate into better multimodal emotion recognition (MER) accuracy, even though it makes predictions more interpretable. Specifically, for reasoning-based MLLMs, fast thinking by triggering direct answers often outperforms slow thinking after deliberative reasoning. Our empirical analyses show that fast thinking improves recall with broader and more confident predictions, whereas slow thinking favors precision through conservative filtering of incorrect categories. Building on these insights, we propose MER-R1, a reinforcement learning framework that turns slow-fast complementarity into explicit optimization. Dual-objective disentanglement separates recall and precision into two optimization signals, allowing them to be jointly optimized rather than traded off against each other. Slow-fast confidence calibration further aligns the final slow-thinking answer with fast-thinking intuition, strengthening correct emotions while suppressing incorrect ones. In this way, MER-R1 unifies the recall-oriented intuition of fast thinking with the precision-oriented selectivity of slow thinking. We further provide theoretical justification for this synergy, showing that it mitigates variance-induced interference during optimization. Extensive experiments on MER-UniBench and MME-Emotion show that MER-R1 achieves state-of-the-art performance and makes reasoning genuinely benefit emotion recognition.

</details>

*Xinyuan Song,Zekun Cai*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种面向图世界模型（GWM）的长时域展开误差分析方法，并设计了误差感知GWM（Error-Aware GWM），通过谱正则化、展开一致性和关键节点加权，有效防止了动态图场景下的长时域发散。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多规划环境以图形式存在（如智能体、工具、技能、路径和依赖关系图），而传统世界模型主要针对向量或图像数据。图世界模型中的局部预测误差可能通过图结构传播放大，且边是动态预测的而非固定的，导致误差累积模式复杂，现有研究缺乏对这一问题的理论分析和解决方案。

Method: 1. 提出了统一框架，涵盖固定边和动态边GWM，包含用于节点级、边级和图级决策的动作节点。2. 推导了图值展开误差界，将拓扑导致的放大与模型导致的放大分离。3. 引入了用于动态边展开的联合节点-边算子。4. 设计了Error-Aware GWM，结合谱正则化、展开一致性和关键节点加权。

Abstract: World models are often used for planning by rolling learned dynamics forward. Many planning environments, however, are not vectors or images; they are graphs of agents, tools, skills, routes, and dependencies. In these settings, a local prediction error may stay local or spread through the graph, and the failure mode changes again when edges are predicted rather than fixed. This paper studies long-horizon rollout error in Graph World Models (GWMs). We formulate a unified fixed-edge and dynamic-edge GWM framework with action nodes for node-, edge-, and graph-level decisions. We develop graph-valued rollout bounds that separate topology-induced amplification from model-induced amplification, and we introduce a joint node-edge operator for dynamic-edge rollouts. Guided by the analysis, we propose Error-Aware GWM, which combines spectral regularization, rollout consistency, and critical-node weighting. Across synthetic topologies and heterogeneous agent-graph testbeds, rollout error and planning regret grow with horizon, dynamic-edge training is needed when structure evolves, and Error-Aware GWM prevents long-horizon divergence while preserving prediction accuracy. Real-world graph benchmarks clarify the scope of GWMs: they are most useful for dynamic graph rollout and agent planning, while specialized graph models remain strong on static or sparse prediction tasks.

### [174] [Grounded Iterative Language Planning: How Parameterized World Models Reduce Hallucination Propagation in LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27806)
*Xinyuan Song,Zekun Cai*

TL;DR: 本文提出GILP方法，通过结合小型参数化世界模型（提供有效动作、状态变化预测等）与LLM代理推理，并引入一致性门控机制，在四个图规划基准上将幻觉状态率从0.176降至0.035，成功率从0.668提升至0.838，仅增加约22%的LLM调用量。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出GILP框架：1）训练小型参数化骨干网络，输出有效动作、状态变化预测、风险和价值；2）LLM代理根据当前状态草拟动作和想象的状态变化；3）设计一致性门控机制，当LLM输出与骨干网络预测不一致时要求修订。在四个图结构规划基准上，使用GPT-4o-mini进行实验。

Result: 在真实GPT-4o-mini调用中，GILP将幻觉状态率从0.176降至0.035；在消融实验中，成功率从0.668提升至0.838，仅增加约22%的额外LLM调用开销。

Conclusion: 通过小型参数化模型与LLM代理的协同工作，并引入一致性验证机制，可以有效降低基于LLM的世界模型的幻觉率，同时显著提升规划成功率，且额外计算开销可控。

Abstract: World models for language agents come in two useful forms. An agent-based world model calls an LLM API and reasons flexibly in language, but its errors appear as hallucinated state changes that are hard to score with ordinary regression losses. A parameterized world model is a trained transition predictor; its errors are easier to measure with quantities such as NodeMSE, delta accuracy, and validity accuracy, but it is usually weaker as a standalone planner. We compare these two families on four graph-structured planning benchmarks and introduce operational hallucination metrics for the agent-based case. The comparison motivates \textbf{Grounded Iterative Language Planning} (GILP), which trains only a small parameterized backbone and combines it with API-based agent reasoning. The backbone supplies valid actions, predicted state deltas, risk, and value; the LLM drafts an action and imagined delta; and a consistency gate asks for revision when the two disagree. On real GPT-4o-mini calls, GILP reduces hallucinated-state rate from 0.176 to 0.035. In calibrated simulator ablations, it raises success from 0.668 to 0.838 while adding only ~22% extra LLM calls.

Consequently, they fall short: a fully aligned agent remains highly vulnerable to runtime hijacking via memory poisoning, tool-chain manipulation, or multi-agent protocol attacks. To address this critical gap, we introduce the Agent-Native Immune System (ANIS), the first biologically inspired, endogenous defense architecture embedded directly within the agent's cognitive loop. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: (1) 退火式OPD-RL调度：早期以OPD为主快速接近教师水平，逐步增强RL推动探索；(2) Turn-level Disagreement-Uncertainty Reweighting (T-DUR)：对长轨迹中高价值回合进行软放大。

Reinforcement learning (RL) directly optimizes environment rewards and encourages exploratory improvement toward a higher reward-defined ceiling, but sparse and delayed feedback makes early-stage learning much less efficient than OPD. In this paper, we propose ATOD (Annealed Turn-aware On-policy Distillation), a hybrid online distillation algorithm that explicitly exploits this complementarity. (1) ATOD uses an annealed OPD-RL schedule: OPD dominates early training to approach teacher-level behavior, while RL is gradually strengthened to drive reward-based exploration. (2) ATOD introduces Turn-level Disagreement-Uncertainty Reweighting (T-DUR), which softly amplifies high-utility turns and improves dense supervision in long trajectories. Experiments on ALFWorld, WebShop, and Search-QA show that ATOD consistently outperforms competing post-training baselines: across the three student sizes, ATOD improves average success rate by 3.03 points over OPD and 23.62 points over GRPO, while surpassing the corresponding teacher models by 2.16 points.

To address this, we propose NormPerceptor, a context-conditioned cue generator that infers scene-relevant norms prior to planning, increasing Task Success from 24.2\% to 46.7\%.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有KGC模型如RotatE和Rotate3D无法同时建模非交换组合、语义层次结构以及一对多等多基数关系。

Method: 提出RelBall模型：(1) 引入模变换建模层次结构，抽象概念模值小，具体实例模值大；(2) 引入以尾实体为中心的关系球，建模一对一、一对多、多对一、多对多关系。

Result: 在多个数据集上的链接预测实验显示，RelBall在性能上优于多种基线模型。

Conclusion: RelBall同时覆盖了对称、反对称、逆、组合、语义层次等所有关系模式，并提供可解释的层次化表示，有效支持多种基数关系。

Abstract: Real-world knowledge graphs are often incomplete, lacking many valid facts. Knowledge Graph Completion (KGC) aims to predict missing links using known triples, thereby enhancing graph coverage. A key challenge is modeling diverse relational patterns such as symmetry, antisymmetry, inversion, composition and semantic hierarchy. Existing models such as RotatE can capture symmetric, antisymmetric, inverse, and commutative composition patterns, yet struggle with non-commutative composition. Rotate3D addresses this by introducing non-commutativity via three-dimensional rotations, but still fails to capture the semantic hierarchies prevalent in knowledge graphs. Moreover, both models cannot effectively model one-to-many relations. To overcome these limitations, we propose RelBall, which extends Rotate3D with two innovations. First, our model introduces modulus transformation to model hierarchies, driving abstract concepts toward smaller moduli and concrete instances toward larger ones. Second, it introduces a tail-centric relation ball to model one-to-one, one-to-many, many-to-one, and many-to-many relations. RelBall offers the following advantages: (1) coverage of all relational patterns, including the ones mentioned above; (2) an interpretable hierarchical representation where the modulus directly reflect semantic levels; (3) support for one-to-one, one-to-many, many-to-one, and many-to-many relations. Experiments on multiple datasets demonstrate RelBall's competitive link prediction performance against various baselines.

</details>

*Malte Luttermann,Tanya Braun,Ralf Möller,Marcel Gehrke*

Main category: cs.AI

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出参数化因果因子图（PCFG）融入因果知识并定义干预的形式语义；设计提升因果推理（LCI）算法在提升层面计算因果效应；进一步提出部分有向PCFG（PD-PCFG）处理部分因果知识，并扩展LCI算法。

Abstract: Lifted inference exploits indistinguishabilities in probabilistic graphical models by using a representative for indistinguishable objects, thereby speeding up query answering while maintaining exact answers. In this article, we show how lifting can be applied to efficiently compute causal effects in relational domains. More specifically, we introduce parametric causal factor graphs (PCFGs) to incorporate causal knowledge in lifted models and give a formal semantics of interventions therein. We further present the Lifted Causal Inference (LCI) algorithm to compute causal effects on a lifted level, thereby drastically speeding up causal inference compared to propositional inference, e.g., in causal Bayesian networks. In addition, we present partially directed parametric causal factor graphs (PD-PCFGs) as a generalisation of PCFGs to handle partial causal knowledge and extend LCI to perform lifted causal inference in a PD-PCFG, thereby extending the applicability of lifted causal inference to a broader range of models requiring less prior knowledge about causal relationships.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于主题中心扩展的多跳KGQA方法面临两个挑战：搜索空间随噪声混合类型路径快速增长，以及检索路径可能无法满足复杂问题的语义约束。

Method: 构建关系中心本体图捕获头尾实体类型约束；采用双向检索机制（主题侧前缀扩展+答案侧最后一跳匹配）；迭代精炼策略重新评估检索路径和候选答案。

Abstract: Knowledge graph question answering (KGQA) aims to answer natural-language questions by reasoning over structured facts. To address these challenges, we propose OPI, an ontology-guided evidence path inference framework for multi-hop KGQA. OPI introduces a relation-centric ontology graph to capture the head-tail type constraints of relations, providing a compact interface for answer-side constraints. Based on this ontology graph, OPI first introduces a bidirectional retrieval mechanism by mapping the predicted answer type to compatible final-hop relations and combining topic-side prefix expansion with answer-side final-hop matching, thereby suppressing noisy mixed-type expansion. OPI further adopts an iterative refinement strategy to reassess retrieved paths and candidate answers under the question context, filtering type-compatible but question-irrelevant evidence for more reliable answer prediction. Experiments on WebQSP, CWQ, and MetaQA show that OPI substantially reduces the search space, improves Hit@1/F1 by 4.6/5.0 points on WebQSP and 8.9/3.3 points on CWQ over the strongest prior results, and achieves near-saturated Hit@1 on MetaQA with the retrieval module alone.

### [184] [Tandem Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28166)
*Difan Jiao,Raghav Singhal,Robert West,Ashton Anderson*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出Tandem Reinforcement Learning (TRL)，将 tandem training 范式扩展到基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）中。TRL 通过让强模型（senior）与冻结的弱模型（junior）交替协同生成推理链，在保持强模型独立推理能力的同时，显著提升了与弱模型协作的鲁棒性、减少了分布漂移，并生成了更易于弱模型理解的推理链，在竞赛数学任务上验证了有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RLVR 虽然大幅提升了 LLM 的推理能力，但其推理过程趋向于可读性差、语言混杂等特殊模式，导致弱模型或人类难以理解和跟随。现有 tandem training 范式虽能解决兼容性问题，但仅在概念验证层面被展示，尚未在长链推理的现代 RLVR 管线中验证其可扩展性。

Method: 提出 Tandem Reinforcement Learning (TRL)，核心机制是：一个可训练的强模型（senior）与一个冻结的弱模型（junior）以随机交替方式共同生成推理过程，生成的推理链获得奖励后，对 senior 应用标准 GRPO 损失进行更新。在 Qwen3-4B-Instruct 模型上以竞赛数学为任务进行训练。

Result: TRL 在独立推理能力上与 vanilla GRPO 持平，同时从同一 rollout 结构中涌现出三个特性：与 junior 更强的交接鲁棒性、减少来自 junior 的分布漂移、以及生成更易于 junior 理解的推理链。

Conclusion: TRL 为 RLVR 提供了一条有前景的路径，在多模型通信和人类兼容性方面具有实际价值。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has significantly improved the reasoning capability of large language models, reaching expert or even superhuman performance in domains such as competition math. However, whether weaker agents and humans can actually harness this capability is far less certain, with RLVR documented to drift reasoning toward idiosyncratic patterns such as poor readability and language mixing. Tandem training is a recently introduced paradigm that targets this compatibility problem: a trained, stronger senior co-generates each rollout with a frozen, weaker junior, and the two are rewarded as a team, so the senior is pushed to reason in ways the junior can follow. Yet this paradigm has so far been demonstrated only in proof-of-concept settings, leaving open whether it scales to the long chains of thought of the modern RLVR pipeline. In this work, we propose Tandem Reinforcement Learning (TRL), which carries the tandem training paradigm into RLVR. In TRL, the senior and a frozen junior alternate stochastically to co-generate the reasoning, the resulting generation is rewarded, and the standard GRPO loss is applied to the senior. Training Qwen3-4B-Instruct on competition math, we find that TRL matches vanilla GRPO on solo reasoning capability while three properties emerge together from the same rollout structure: stronger handoff robustness with the junior, reduced distributional drift from the junior, and a chain-of-thought more legible to the junior. Our results demonstrate a promising route for RLVR with practical payoffs in multi-model communication and human compatibility.

</details>

We introduce SidConArena, a new benchmark framework for evaluating LLM agents in open-ended, positive-sum bargaining. The framework combines structured observations, phase-aware agent dispatching, a neural-symbolic action interface, and asynchronous execution, enabling free-form interaction while preserving rule-grounded evaluation. ### [186] [Delayed Verification Destabilizes Multi-Agent LLM Belief: Instability Thresholds and Optimal Corrector Placement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27409)
*Igor Itkin*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文研究了多智能体LLM系统中验证延迟导致的事实性振荡问题，通过谱图理论建立了稳定性阈值，并提出了最优纠正资源分配策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体LLM系统中，验证器/批评者智能体用于抑制幻觉，但验证存在延迟，导致错误信息在延迟期间在网络中传播，引发系统不稳定。

Method: 将验证延迟建模为图上带接地修正节点的延迟共识过程；利用接地拉普拉斯矩阵谱分解推导验证剂量的闭式稳定性阈值；提出超模放置目标和贪心(1-1/e)近似分配规则。

Result: 发现通信延迟与验证延迟重合时最不稳定；延迟为2时阈值为黄金分割比的倒数；实验在5个开源模型上验证了剂量-延迟振荡现象；接地事实回答使真相成为吸收边界从而消除振荡。

Conclusion: 验证延迟导致的振荡现象是符号信念任务特有的，而接地验证（事实性回答）具有稳定作用，为设计更稳定的多智能体LLM系统提供了理论指导。

Abstract: Multi-agent large language model (LLM) systems often rely on verifier and critic agents to suppress hallucinations, but verification is delayed. During this delay, false claims can propagate through the agent network. We model this process as delayed consensus on a graph with grounded corrector nodes. Spectral decomposition by the grounded Laplacian yields a closed-form stability threshold for the verification dose: correction that is too strong or too delayed can turn consensus into oscillation. The most unstable regime occurs when the communication and verification delays coincide; for delay two, the threshold is the inverse golden ratio. The same framework gives a supermodular placement objective and a greedy (1-1/e)-approximation rule for assigning a limited corrector budget to influential nodes. Experiments across five open models confirm the predicted dose-delay oscillations. By contrast, grounded factual answering makes truth an absorbing boundary and eliminates the effect, suggesting that the instability is specific to signed-belief tasks while grounded verification remains stabilizing

### [187] [Glite ARF: Verifier-Driven Research with Parallel LLM Coding Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27416)
*Vassili Philippov,Pavel Katunin,Dmitry Andreev,Igor Ostanin,Anton Nikolaev*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 提出了Glite ARF框架，通过验证器驱动的三角色协作机制（人类研究者+LLM编码代理+确定性验证器），在保证可复现性和可审计性的前提下实现大规模并行自动化实验研究，并在BEA 2026词汇难度共享任务中取得领先成绩。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 直接将LLM编码代理用于自动化实证研究时，微小的指令失误会累积成无法复现的混乱结果，大型项目中这种问题尤为突出，需要一种可扩展且保证可复现性和可审计性的解决方案。

Method: 提出三角色堆栈：人类研究者选择假设，LLM编码代理（Claude Code, Codex CLI）在固定结构下执行任务，确定性Python验证器脚本执行任务隔离、已完成工作不可变性、修正覆盖层和项目概览物化。核心思想是将研究规则编码为可执行代码而非自然语言指令。

Result: 在BEA 2026词汇难度共享任务中，封闭赛道第一、开放赛道第二，三个目标语言上官方基线RMSE降低29.9%（封闭）和35.9%（开放）；273个追踪任务、146次实验运行、129个特征集、最多12个并行代理，总第三方成本约498美元；框架额外开销仅约1%的挂钟时间。

Conclusion: 验证器驱动的研究范式（verifier-driven research）能够有效解决LLM编码代理在大规模自动化研究中的可靠性问题，框架轻量且跨领域适用，实现了可审计、可复现的大规模并行实验。

Abstract: LLM coding agents make it tempting to automate empirical research by delegating experiments to them directly, but naive delegation does not scale to large projects: low-rate instruction lapses compound into broken, irreproducible artefacts. To address this problem, we present Glite ARF, an open-source Python framework for running many LLM coding agents in parallel on a research repository without sacrificing reproducibility or auditability. The framework defines a three-role stack: a human researcher chooses which hypotheses to test, coding agents (Claude Code, Codex CLI) implement individual tasks under a fixed structure, and deterministic Python verifier scripts enforce task isolation, immutability of completed work, a corrections overlay, and a materialised project overview. We call this verifier-driven research: the rules of the research process live in code that fails loudly when violated, not in prose that agents are merely asked to follow. Using Glite ARF, we developed our submission to the BEA 2026 vocabulary-difficulty shared task, placing first in the closed track and second in the open track on all three target languages (Spanish, German, Mandarin) and reducing the official baseline RMSE by 29.9% (closed) and 35.9% (open). The campaign comprised 273 tracked tasks (146 experiment runs) across 129 feature sets, run by up to twelve parallel agents orchestrated from a single laptop - with some model training on rented A100s - at approximately \$450 in LLM API spend (\$498 total third-party cost), and structured per-fold provenance let us catch and strip four target-leaking feature sets, correcting an implausible 0.609 RMSE to 0.802. Across three campaigns in three domains, the framework's structural machinery adds only about 1% of wall-clock time. Framework and a public demo project accompany this paper.

</details>


### [188] [QueenBee Planner: Skill-Evolving Communication Topologies for Token-Efficient LLM Multi-Agent Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27492)
*Congjia Tian,Yuhang Yao,Jiaming Cui*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: QueenBee Planner：一种将多智能体通信拓扑视为可检索、自改进设计技能的外层LLM规划器框架，通过证据驱动的设计规则（保留/修改/避免）和多种防过拟合机制，在固定底层模型的情况下自进化生成通信DAG，显著优于固定拓扑和冷生成基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM多智能体系统越来越依赖智能体间的连接方式，但通信拓扑通常由人工设计或固定不变，缺乏自动优化和可重用的设计知识。

Method: QueenBee Planner：外层LLM学习生成时序通信DAG（谁向谁发送信息、第几轮、谁合并消息、谁输出最终答案）；将执行轨迹蒸馏为证据支持的设计规则（Preserve/Modify/Avoid）；采用held-out acceptance gates、variance-aware credit、motif-level attribution、transfer trust、insight falsification、structural deduplication等机制防止自我进化过拟合。

Result: 在Count-Frequency聚合任务中，最佳生成图将RMSE从固定拓扑最优的12.53降至7.87，同时减少消息数、模型调用和token成本；Silo-Bench分布式协调任务也显示相同改进方向。

Conclusion: 多智能体系统可以学习可重用的架构设计知识，而不仅仅是记忆任务答案。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) multi-agent systems increasingly depend not only on how individual agents reason, but also on how agents are connected. This paper introduces QueenBee Planner, a framework that treats inter-agent communication topology as a retrievable and self-improving design skill. A pool of worker agents, the task adapter, and the scoring function are frozen; only an outer LLM planner learns to generate temporal communication DAGs specifying who sends information to whom, in which round, who merges messages, and who emits the final answer. Execution traces are distilled into evidence-backed design rules with three actions: \emph{Preserve}, \emph{Modify}, and \emph{Avoid}. To prevent self-evolution from turning lucky runs or plausible but false explanations into policy, QueenBee uses held-out acceptance gates, variance-aware credit, motif-level attribution, transfer trust, insight falsification, and structural deduplication. We evaluate the method on Count-Frequency aggregation and Silo-Bench-style distributed coordination tasks. With fixed workers, self-evolved graph generation produces communication structures that improve over fixed topologies and cold generation. In the CF fulltest setting, the best generated graph reduces RMSE from 12.53 for the strongest fixed topology to 7.87 while also reducing messages, model calls, and token cost; Silo-style results show the same direction of improvement over cold and fixed-topology baselines. These results suggest that multi-agent systems can learn reusable architectural design knowledge rather than merely memorizing task answers.

</details>


### [189] [GenWorld: Empirically Grounded Urban Simulation Infrastructure for Scalable LLM-Agent Studies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27650)
*Gen Li,Jieyuan Lan,Pengcheng Xu,Zongyuan Wu,Masaki Ogura,Tao Feng*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: GenWorld是一个结合建筑级合成城市、结构化智能体-环境接口和离线编译LLM决策信号的城市模拟基础设施，在日本东广岛实现了196,608个合成居民的可扩展模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM智能体模拟面临联合接地（需反映真实城市约束）和扩展（大规模人口在线调用LLM计算成本过高）的双重问题。

Method: 构建建筑级合成城市、结构化智能体-环境接口、将LLM决策信号离线编译为查找策略以实现可扩展推演。

Result: 在日本东广岛实例化196,608个合成居民，通过人口普查数据验证人口统计一致性，利用YJMob100K手机数据作为通勤距离诊断，并展示了全城工作日推演、工作日-周末行为对比和预警响应扰动三个可复现案例。

Conclusion: GenWorld可作为可复现的接地且可扩展的LLM智能体研究平台，但对交通、疏散或政策结果的校准预测仍是未来工作。

Abstract: LLM-agent simulation faces a joint grounding and scaling problem: agents should act in environments that reflect real urban constraints, yet direct online LLM calls for city-scale populations are computationally prohibitive. We present GenWorld, an empirically grounded urban simulation infrastructure that combines a building-level synthetic city, a structured agent-environment interface, and offline compilation of LLM-derived decision signals into lookup policies for scalable rollout. In a reference instantiation for Higashihiroshima, Japan, GenWorld grounds 196,608 synthetic residents in census and geospatial data, validates demographic consistency against census tabulations, and uses YJMob100K mobile-phone data as a commuting-distance diagnostic. We demonstrate the infrastructure through three reproducible cases: a full-city weekday rollout, a weekday-weekend behavioral contrast, and a warning-response perturbation with auditable replanning traces. These cases support GenWorld as a reproducible platform for grounded and scalable LLM-agent studies, while calibrated forecasting for traffic, evacuation, or policy outcomes remains future work.

</details>


### [190] [GBC: Gradient-Based Connections for Optimizing Multi-Agent Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28187)
*Xiaocheng Yang,Abdulrahman Alrabah,Dilek Hakkani-Tür,Gokhan Tur*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出GBC方法，通过将多智能体系统建模为计算图并引入基于梯度的连接权重，实现token级别的细粒度归因和优化，显著提升多智能体系统性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于LLM的多智能体系统因缺乏细粒度信用分配而性能受限，粗粒度反馈难以定位错误来源。

Method: 将MAS建模为计算图，引入梯度连接权重量化智能体输出对下游的token级影响；构建归因图反向传播损失信号，实现精准归因与定向提示优化；开发AgentChord高效实现。

Result: 在MultiWOZ和τ-bench上超过强基线，归因质量越高优化效果越好。

Conclusion: GBC有效解决多智能体系统的信用分配问题，通过细粒度归因和优化提升整体性能。

Abstract: Multi-agent systems (MAS) built on large language models (LLMs) provide a promising framework for solving complex tasks through role specialization and structured interaction. However, their performance is often limited by miscoordination and, more fundamentally, the lack of fine-grained credit assignment across agents. Existing approaches typically rely on coarse-grained feedback, making it difficult to identify which agents or interaction steps are responsible for errors. We propose Gradient-Based Connections (GBC), an approach for fine-grained attribution and optimization of multi-agent systems. GBC models a MAS as a computational graph and introduces gradient-based connection weights to quantify the influence of each agent's output on downstream agents at the token level. By constructing an attribution graph and propagating task-specific loss signals backward, our method enables precise identification of error sources and targeted prompt optimization. We further develop AgentChord, an efficient implementation that leverages prefix-based gradient computation. Experiments on MultiWOZ and τ-bench show that GBC improves multi-agent performance and outperforms strong single-agent and multi-agent baselines, and higher attribution quality is associated with greater optimization effectiveness. Code is available at: https://github.com/yxc-cyber/AgentChord.

</details>
